# Single-cell and Spatial Omics Techniques from LinkedIn Posts

Curated handbook of tools, techniques, methods, frameworks, and experimental technologies identified from the LinkedIn posts CSV.

Links that were already present in the CSV are shown without provenance labels. Only resources added externally, when present, are marked as `External — not present in CSV`.

# Index

## Single-cell RNA-seq
- Experimental Technologies
- Preprocessing & Quality Control
- Normalization & Batch Integration
- Dimensionality Reduction & Clustering
- Cell Type Annotation
- Differential Expression & Marker Discovery
- Trajectory Inference & Pseudotime
- RNA Velocity
- Gene Regulatory Network Inference
- Cell–Cell Communication
- Functional Enrichment & Pathway Analysis
- Multimodal Integration
- Simulation & Benchmarking
- Visualization & Interactive Exploration

## Spatial Omics
- Experimental Technologies
- Preprocessing & Quality Control
- Cell Segmentation
- Spatial Cell Type Annotation
- Spatial Differential Expression

- Spatial Domains & Tissue Architecture
- Spatial Cell–Cell Communication
- Neighborhood & Microenvironment Analysis
- Colocalization & Spatial Pattern Analysis
- Multi-sample Spatial Integration
- Visualization & Interactive Exploration

## Single-cell & Spatial Integration
- Reference-based Deconvolution
- Cell Mapping & Label Transfer
- Spatial Cell Mapping & Reconstruction
- Probabilistic Integration

# Single-cell RNA-seq

## Experimental Technologies

### FixNCut

FixNCut is an experimental technology for generating single-cell or spatial omics measurements.

- **Categories**: - Single-cell RNA-seq → Experimental Technologies

- **Repositories / resources**: - Website: https://buff.ly/3vBBo9O

RoCK and ROI performs pathway or functional enrichment analysis for single-cell omics data.

- **Paper**: - https://doi.org/10.1038/s41467-025-66248-z

### scRepli‑RamDA‑seq (scRR‑seq)

- **Paper**: - https://doi.org/10.64898/2026.01.13.699237
